     1â†’#!/usr/bin/env node
     2â†’
     3â†’/**
     4â†’ * Prompt Override Parser - UserPromptSubmit Hook
     5â†’ *
     6â†’ * Parses user prompts for OVERRIDE_CONSTRAINT directives and stores them
     7â†’ * for the PreTool hook to consume.
     8â†’ *
     9â†’ * Usage in prompt:
    10â†’ *   OVERRIDE_CONSTRAINT: constraint-id-1
    11â†’ *   OVERRIDE_CONSTRAINT: constraint-id-2
    12â†’ *
    13â†’ * Creates temporary state file: /tmp/constraint-override-{pid}.json
    14â†’ */
    15â†’
    16â†’import { readFileSync, writeFileSync, existsSync } from 'fs';
    17â†’import { tmpdir } from 'os';
    18â†’import { join } from 'path';
    19â†’
    20â†’async function parsePromptForOverrides() {
    21â†’  try {
    22â†’    // Read prompt from stdin
    23â†’    let promptData = '';
    24â†’
    25â†’    if (process.stdin.isTTY !== true) {
    26â†’      const chunks = [];
    27â†’      for await (const chunk of process.stdin) {
    28â†’        chunks.push(chunk);
    29â†’      }
    30â†’      if (chunks.length > 0) {
    31â†’        promptData = Buffer.concat(chunks).toString('utf8');
    32â†’      }
    33â†’    }
    34â†’
    35â†’    if (!promptData) {
    36â†’      // No prompt data - exit silently
    37â†’      process.exit(0);
    38â†’    }
    39â†’
    40â†’    let userPrompt;
    41â†’    try {
    42â†’      const data = JSON.parse(promptData);
    43â†’      userPrompt = data.prompt || data.message || data.content || promptData;
    44â†’    } catch {
    45â†’      // If not JSON, treat entire input as prompt
    46â†’      userPrompt = promptData;
    47â†’    }
    48â†’
    49â†’    // Parse OVERRIDE_CONSTRAINT directives
    50â†’    const overridePattern = /OVERRIDE_CONSTRAINT:\s*([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)/g;
    51â†’    const matches = [...userPrompt.matchAll(overridePattern)];
    52â†’
    53â†’    if (matches.length === 0) {
    54â†’      // No overrides requested - exit silently
    55â†’      process.exit(0);
    56â†’    }
    57â†’
    58â†’    // Extract constraint IDs
    59â†’    const constraintIds = matches.map(m => m[1]);
    60â†’
    61â†’    // Create override state file
    62â†’    const sessionId = process.env.CLAUDE_SESSION_ID || process.ppid || Date.now();
    63â†’    const stateFile = join(tmpdir(), `constraint-override-${sessionId}.json`);
    64â†’
    65â†’    const overrideState = {
    66â†’      constraintIds,
    67â†’      createdAt: Date.now(),
    68â†’      expiresAt: Date.now() + (5 * 60 * 1000), // 5 minutes TTL
    69â†’      promptCount: 0,
    70â†’      maxPrompts: 3 // Expire after 3 prompts
    71â†’    };
    72â†’
    73â†’    writeFileSync(stateFile, JSON.stringify(overrideState, null, 2));
    74â†’
    75â†’    // Output informational message for user context (hooks CAN output to stderr on exit 0)
    76â†’    console.error(`âœ… Constraint override active for: ${constraintIds.join(', ')}`);
    77â†’    console.error(`   Valid for 3 prompts or 5 minutes`);
    78â†’
    79â†’    process.exit(0);
    80â†’
    81â†’  } catch (error) {
    82â†’    // Fail open - don't block on errors
    83â†’    console.error('âš ï¸ Override parser error:', error.message);
    84â†’    process.exit(0);
    85â†’  }
    86â†’}
    87â†’
    88â†’parsePromptForOverrides();
    89â†’

     1â†’#!/usr/bin/env node
     2â†’
     3â†’/**
     4â†’ * Real-Time Constraint Enforcement Hook
     5â†’ * 
     6â†’ * This hook intercepts every user prompt and tool call to check for constraint violations
     7â†’ * BEFORE execution. If violations are detected, it blocks execution and requires correction.
     8â†’ * 
     9â†’ * Usage: Called by Claude Code hook system on every interaction
    10â†’ */
    11â†’
    12â†’import { readFileSync, existsSync } from 'fs';
    13â†’import { join, dirname } from 'path';
    14â†’import { fileURLToPath } from 'url';
    15â†’import { execSync } from 'child_process';
    16â†’import { logger } from '../utils/logger.js';
    17â†’
    18â†’const __filename = fileURLToPath(import.<COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED>.url);
    19â†’const __dirname = dirname(__filename);
    20â†’
    21â†’class RealTimeConstraintEnforcer {
    22â†’  constructor() {
    23â†’    this.projectPath = process.env.PWD || process.cwd();
    24â†’    this.constraintConfigPath = this.findConstraintConfig();
    25â†’    this.config = this.loadConfig();
    26â†’    // Direct constraint engine integration - no HTTP calls needed
    27â†’  }
    28â†’
    29â†’  findConstraintConfig() {
    30â†’    // Look for project-specific config first, then global
    31â†’    const projectConfig = join(this.projectPath, '.constraint-monitor.yaml');
    32â†’    const globalConfig = join(process.env.CODING_REPO || '', '.constraint-monitor.yaml');
    33â†’    
    34â†’    if (existsSync(projectConfig)) {
    35â†’      return projectConfig;
    36â†’    } else if (existsSync(globalConfig)) {
    37â†’      return globalConfig;
    38â†’    }
    39â†’    return null;
    40â†’  }
    41â†’
    42â†’  loadConfig() {
    43â†’    if (!this.constraintConfigPath) {
    44â†’      return { enforcement: { enabled: false } };
    45â†’    }
    46â†’
    47â†’    try {
    48â†’      // Use the existing constraint engine to load config
    49â†’      const configScript = join(__dirname, '../config/load-constraints.js');
    50â†’      const result = execSync(`node "${configScript}" "${this.constraintConfigPath}"`, {
    51â†’        encoding: 'utf8',
    52â†’        timeout: 3000
    53â†’      });
    54â†’      const config = JSON.parse(result);
    55â†’
    56â†’      // Add default enforcement settings if not present
    57â†’      if (!config.enforcement) {
    58â†’        config.enforcement = {
    59â†’          enabled: true,
    60â†’          blocking_levels: ['critical', 'error'],

    68â†’    } catch (error) {

    70â†’      return { enforcement: { enabled: false } };
    71â†’    }
    72â†’  }
    73â†’
    74â†’  async checkConstraintsDirectly(content, type, context = {}) {
    75â†’    try {
    76â†’      // Use the constraint engine directly instead of HTTP API calls
    77â†’      const { ConstraintEngine } = await import('../engines/constraint-engine.js');
    78â†’      const { ConfigManager } = await import('../utils/config-manager.js');
    79â†’
    80â†’      const configManager = new ConfigManager();

    83â†’

    85â†’        content,
    86â†’        type,
    87â†’        filePath: context.filePath
    88â†’      });
    89â†’

    91â†’    } catch (error) {

    93â†’      return { violations: [], compliance: 10 }; // Fail open
    94â†’    }
    95â†’  }
    96â†’
    97â†’  getProjectName() {
    98â†’    const segments = this.projectPath.split('/');
    99â†’    return segments[segments.length - 1] || 'unknown';
   100â†’  }
   101â†’
   102â†’  shouldBlockViolation(violation, constraintOverride = null) {
   103â†’    const blockingLevels = this.config.enforcement?.blocking_levels || ['critical', 'error'];
   104â†’
   105â†’    // Check if this violation has a user-initiated override
   106â†’    if (constraintOverride) {
   107â†’      const overrideList = Array.isArray(constraintOverride)
   108â†’        ? constraintOverride
   109â†’        : [constraintOverride];
   110â†’
   111â†’      if (overrideList.includes(violation.constraint_id)) {
   112â†’        // Log the override for audit trail
   113â†’        logger.info(`ğŸ”“ CONSTRAINT OVERRIDE: User-initiated override for constraint '${violation.constraint_id}'`);
   114â†’        return false; // Don't block this violation
   115â†’      }
   116â†’    }
   117â†’
   118â†’    return blockingLevels.includes(violation.severity);
   119â†’  }
   120â†’
   121â†’  formatViolationMessage(violations, constraintOverride = null) {
   122â†’    const blockingViolations = violations.filter(v => this.shouldBlockViolation(v, constraintOverride));
   123â†’
   124â†’    // Check if any violations were overridden
   125â†’    const overriddenViolations = violations.filter(v => {
   126â†’      if (!constraintOverride) return false;
   127â†’      const overrideList = Array.isArray(constraintOverride) ? constraintOverride : [constraintOverride];
   128â†’      return overrideList.includes(v.constraint_id) && this.config.enforcement?.blocking_levels?.includes(v.severity);
   129â†’    });
   130â†’
   131â†’    if (blockingViolations.length === 0) {
   132â†’      // If we have overridden violations, log them for user awareness
   133â†’      if (overriddenViolations.length > 0) {
   134â†’        const overriddenIds = overriddenViolations.map(v => v.constraint_id).join(', ');
   135â†’        logger.info(`âœ… Tool allowed with constraint override(s): ${overriddenIds}`);
   136â†’      }
   137â†’      return null; // No blocking violations
   138â†’    }
   139â†’
   140â†’    const lines = [
   141â†’      'ğŸš« **CONSTRAINT VIOLATION DETECTED - EXECUTION BLOCKED**',
   142â†’      '',
   143â†’      'The following constraint violations must be corrected before proceeding:',
   144â†’      ''
   145â†’    ];
   146â†’
   147â†’    blockingViolations.forEach((violation, index) => {
   148â†’      lines.push(`**${index + 1}. ${violation.severity.toUpperCase()}: ${violation.message}**`);
   149â†’      if (violation.suggestion) {
   150â†’        lines.push(`   ğŸ’¡ Suggestion: ${violation.suggestion}`);

   164â†’
   165â†’  async enforcePromptConstraints(prompt, context = {}) {
   166â†’    if (!this.config.enforcement?.enabled) {
   167â†’      return { allowed: true };
   168â†’    }
   169â†’
   170â†’    const checkResult = await this.checkConstraintsDirectly(prompt, 'prompt', context);
   171â†’
   172â†’    // Log ALL violations to dashboard BEFORE deciding whether to block
   173â†’    if (checkResult.violations && checkResult.violations.length > 0) {
   174â†’      await this.logViolationsToStorage(checkResult.violations, context, 'prompt');
   175â†’    }
   176â†’
   177â†’    const blockingMessage = this.formatViolationMessage(checkResult.violations || []);
   178â†’
   179â†’    if (blockingMessage) {
   180â†’      return {
   181â†’        allowed: false,
   182â†’        reason: 'constraint_violation',
   183â†’        message: blockingMessage,
   184â†’        violations: checkResult.violations
   185â†’      };
   186â†’    }
   187â†’
   188â†’    return { allowed: true, compliance: checkResult.compliance };
   189â†’  }
   190â†’
   191â†’  async enforceToolConstraints(toolCall, context = {}) {
   192â†’    if (!this.config.enforcement?.enabled) {
   193â†’      return { allowed: true };
   194â†’    }
   195â†’
   196â†’    // Extract the actual content from tool calls for constraint checking
   197â†’    let contentToCheck = '';
   198â†’    const params = toolCall.parameters || toolCall.arguments || {};
   199â†’
   200â†’    // For Write/Edit tool calls, check the content being written
   201â†’    if (['Write', 'Edit', 'MultiEdit'].includes(toolCall.name)) {
   202â†’      contentToCheck = params.content || params.new_string || '';
   203â†’      // Also check old_string for Edit operations
   204â†’      if (params.old_string) {
   205â†’        contentToCheck += '\n' + params.old_string;
   206â†’      }
   207â†’      // For MultiEdit, check all edits
   208â†’      if (params.edits && Array.isArray(params.edits)) {
   209â†’        params.edits.forEach(edit => {
   210â†’          contentToCheck += '\n' + (edit.new_string || '') + '\n' + (edit.old_string || '');
   211â†’        });
   212â†’      }
   213â†’
   214â†’      // SPECIAL CASE: For file path constraints, also check the file path
   215â†’      if (params.file_path) {
   216â†’        contentToCheck += '\n' + params.file_path;
   217â†’      }
   218â†’    } else {
   219â†’      // For other tools, serialize the entire call
   220â†’      contentToCheck = JSON.stringify({
   221â†’        tool: toolCall.name,
   222â†’        parameters: params,
   223â†’        context: context
   224â†’      }, null, 2);
   225â†’    }
   226â†’
   227â†’    const checkResult = await this.checkConstraintsDirectly(contentToCheck, 'tool_call', context);
   228â†’
   229â†’    // Log ALL violations to dashboard BEFORE deciding whether to block
   230â†’    if (checkResult.violations && checkResult.violations.length > 0) {
   231â†’      await this.logViolationsToStorage(checkResult.violations, { ...context, filePath: params.file_path }, 'tool_call');
   232â†’    }
   233â†’
   234â†’    // Pass constraint override from context to violation formatting
   235â†’    const blockingMessage = this.formatViolationMessage(checkResult.violations || [], context.constraintOverride);
   236â†’
   237â†’    if (blockingMessage) {
   238â†’      return {
   239â†’        allowed: false,
   240â†’        reason: 'constraint_violation',
   241â†’        message: blockingMessage,
   242â†’        violations: checkResult.violations
   243â†’      };
   244â†’    }
   245â†’
   246â†’    return { allowed: true, compliance: checkResult.compliance };
   247â†’  }
   248â†’

    10â†’
    11â†’function loadConstraints(configPath) {

   138â†’
   139â†’### Compliance Score Calculation
   140â†’
   141â†’```javascript
   142â†’function calculateComplianceScore(violations) {
   143â†’  let score = 10.0; // Start perfect
   144â†’
   145â†’  violations.forEach(v => {
   146â†’    switch(v.severity) {
   147â†’      case 'critical': score -= 3.0; break;
   148â†’      case 'error':    score -= 2.0; break;
   149â†’      case 'warning':  score -= 1.0; break;
   150â†’      case 'info':     score -= 0.5; break;
   151â†’    }
   152â†’  });
   153â†’
   154â†’  return Math.max(0, Math.min(10, score));
   155â†’}
   156â†’```

   195â†’### Constraint Overrides
   196â†’
   197â†’The system supports **temporary constraint overrides** for situations where a constraint needs to be bypassed (e.g., fixing the constraint configuration itself, emergency fixes, or legitimate exceptions).
   198â†’
   199â†’#### How to Use Overrides
   200â†’
   201â†’Include `OVERRIDE_CONSTRAINT` directives in your prompt to Claude:
   202â†’
   203â†’```
   204â†’OVERRIDE_CONSTRAINT: constraint-id-1
   205â†’OVERRIDE_CONSTRAINT: constraint-id-2
   206â†’
   207â†’Your actual task description goes here...
   208â†’```
   209â†’
   210â†’**Example**:
   211â†’```
   212â†’OVERRIDE_CONSTRAINT: documentation-style-skill-required
   213â†’OVERRIDE_CONSTRAINT: plantuml-standard-styling
   214â†’
   215â†’Fix the constraint patterns in .constraint-monitor.yaml
   216â†’```
   217â†’
   218â†’#### Override Mechanism
   219â†’
   220â†’1. **UserPromptSubmit Hook** (`prompt-override-parser.js`) detects `OVERRIDE_CONSTRAINT` directives
   221â†’2. Creates temporary state file: `/tmp/constraint-override-{session-id}.json`
   222â†’3. **PreToolUse Hook** reads the state file and bypasses specified constraints
   223â†’4. **Automatic Expiration**: Override expires after:
   224â†’   - **3 prompt sets** (complete request/response cycles), OR
   225â†’   - **5 minutes** (whichever comes first)
   226â†’
   227â†’#### Override State File Format
   228â†’
   229â†’```json
   230â†’{
   231â†’  "constraintIds": [
   232â†’    "documentation-style-skill-required",
   233â†’    "plantuml-standard-styling"
   234â†’  ],
   235â†’  "createdAt": 1763282756000,
   236â†’  "expiresAt": 1763283056000,
   237â†’  "promptCount": 0,
   238â†’  "maxPrompts": 3
   239â†’}
   240â†’```
   241â†’
   242â†’#### Session ID Resolution
   243â†’
   244â†’The override mechanism uses **session ID** to track which session the override applies to:
   245â†’
   246â†’1. `CLAUDE_SESSION_ID` environment variable (if set)
   247â†’2. `process.ppid` (parent process ID) as fallback
   248â†’3. `'default'` as final fallback
   249â†’
   250â†’âš ï¸ **Important**: Overrides are session-specific and will not carry over to new sessions.
   251â†’
   252â†’#### When to Use Overrides
   253â†’
   254â†’âœ… **Legitimate uses**:
   255â†’- Fixing constraint configuration files (<COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED>-editing)
   256â†’- Emergency hotfixes that violate patterns temporarily
   257â†’- Documented exceptions for specific scenarios
   258â†’- Testing constraint behavior
   259â†’
   260â†’âŒ **DON'T abuse overrides for**:
   261â†’- Avoiding proper refactoring
   262â†’- Bypassing security constraints without justification
   263â†’- Creating parallel versions or evolutionary naming
   264â†’- Permanent workarounds
   265â†’
   266â†’#### Audit Trail
   267â†’
   268â†’All override usage is logged for audit purposes:
   269â†’
   270â†’```

### âœ… Tasks Completed

   - **Now only triggers on**:
     - PlantUML/Mermaid code blocks: `` ```plantuml ``, `` ```mermaid ``
     - PlantUML directives: `@startuml`
     - Mermaid diagram syntax: `flowchart`, `sequenceDiagram`
   - âœ… Verified with pattern tests - no false positives on content keywords

   - Added whitelist for:
     - `*.yaml`
     - `*.yml`  
     - `.constraint-monitor.yaml`

     1â†’# UKB - Update Knowledge Base
     2â†’
     3â†’**Component**: [ukb-cli](../../lib/knowledge-api/)
     4â†’**Type**: Command-line tool (Node.js)
     5â†’**Purpose**: Capture and manage development insights
     6â†’
     7â†’---
     8â†’
     9â†’## Overview
    10â†’
    11â†’UKB-CLI is a modern Node.js-based knowledge management system that captures, analyzes, and organizes technical knowledge across projects. It provides intelligent knowledge capture through automatic git analysis and interactive prompts.
    12â†’
    13â†’![UKB Fallback Knowledge Capture Workflow](../images/fallback-knowledge-capture.png)
    14â†’
    15â†’The UKB system provides a manual fallback mechanism for knowledge capture when automated systems are unavailable or insufficient. It supports both automatic git-based analysis and interactive modes for capturing insights.
    16â†’
    17â†’### Key Features
    18â†’
    19â†’- **Cross-Platform**: Pure Node.js with no OS-specific dependencies
    20â†’- **Intelligent Git Analysis**: Incremental commit processing with pattern detection
    21â†’- **Interactive Mode**: Guided prompts with real-time validation
    22â†’- **<USER_ID_REDACTED> Assurance**: Content filtering and URL validation
    23â†’- **Agent Integration**: Programmatic API for coding agents
    24â†’- **MCP Synchronization**: Automatic memory graph updates
    25â†’
    26â†’---
    27â†’
    28â†’## Quick Reference
    29â†’
    30â†’### Basic Commands
    31â†’
    32â†’```bash
    33â†’# Auto-analysis mode (incremental git analysis)
    34â†’ukb
    35â†’
    36â†’# Interactive deep insight capture
    37â†’ukb --interactive
    38â†’
    39â†’# List all entities
    40â†’ukb --list-entities
    41â†’
    42â†’# Search knowledge base
    43â†’ukb search "pattern name"
    44â†’
    45â†’# Add specific entity
    46â†’ukb --add-entity "EntityName" --type TransferablePattern
    47â†’```
    48â†’
    49â†’### Interactive Mode
    50â†’
    51â†’```bash
    52â†’ukb --interactive
    53â†’
    54â†’# Enhanced prompts with validation:
    55â†’# - Problem description (with content filtering)
    56â†’# - Solution approach (with implementation details)
    57â†’# - Rationale for the solution
    58â†’# - Key learnings and insights
    59â†’# - Applicability context
    60â†’# - Technologies used (validated list)
    61â†’# - Reference URLs (automatically verified)
    62â†’# - Related code files
    63â†’# - Custom entity naming support
    64â†’```
    65â†’

    67â†’
    68â†’## Usage Modes
    69â†’
    70â†’### 1. Auto Mode (Default) - Intelligent Git Analysis
    71â†’
    72â†’```bash
    73â†’ukb
    74â†’```
    75â†’
    76â†’**What it does:**
    77â†’- Analyzes recent git commits for patterns
    78â†’- Incremental processing to avoid duplicate work
    79â†’- Automatic pattern detection with significance scoring
    80â†’- Categorizes commits (feature, fix, refactor, etc.)
    81â†’- Updates knowledge base automatically
    82â†’
    83â†’**Use when:**
    84â†’- End of development session
    85â†’- After implementing significant changes
    86â†’- Daily knowledge accumulation
    87â†’- Automated CI/CD integration
    88â†’
    89â†’### 2. Interactive Mode - Structured Capture
    90â†’
    91â†’```bash
    92â†’ukb --interactive
    93â†’```
    94â†’
    95â†’**What it does:**
    96â†’- Structured problem-solution-rationale capture
    97â†’- Real-time URL verification for reference links
    98â†’- Custom entity naming support
    99â†’- Technology validation against known frameworks
   100â†’- Content <USER_ID_REDACTED> filters
   101â†’
   102â†’**Use when:**
   103â†’- Documenting architectural decisions
   104â†’- Capturing complex solutions
   105â†’- Recording lessons learned
   106â†’- Deep insight capture
   107â†’
   108â†’### 3. Search and Query
   109â†’
   110â†’```bash
   111â†’# Search by keyword
   112â†’ukb search "authentication pattern"
   113â†’
   114â†’# List entities by type
   115â†’ukb --list-entities --type TransferablePattern
   116â†’
   117â†’# Show specific entity details
   118â†’ukb entity show "ReactHookPattern" --verbose
   119â†’```
   120â†’
   121â†’### 4. Management Operations
   122â†’
   123â†’```bash
   124â†’# Remove entity
   125â†’ukb --remove-entity "EntityName"
   126â†’
   127â†’# Rename entity

   129â†’
   130â†’# Remove relation

   132â†’
   133â†’# Validate knowledge base

   135â†’
   136â†’# Export knowledge base

   140â†’---
   141â†’
   142â†’## Architecture
   143â†’
   144â†’### Modern Node.js Design
   145â†’
   146â†’UKB-CLI follows a layered architecture:
   147â†’
   148â†’- **CLI Layer**: Command-line interface with comprehensive argument parsing
   149â†’- **Core Services**: Knowledge management, git analysis, and insight extraction
   150â†’- **Validation Layer**: Content <USER_ID_REDACTED> assurance and schema compliance
   151â†’- **Integration Layer**: MCP synchronization and visualizer updates
   152â†’
   153â†’### Backward Compatibility
   154â†’
   155â†’100% backward compatible with legacy bash UKB:
   156â†’- All existing `ukb` commands work unchanged
   157â†’- Legacy script preserved as `ukb-original`
   158â†’- Transparent delegation to Node.js implementation
   159â†’- Same data format and git integration
   160â†’
   161â†’---
   162â†’
   163â†’## Knowledge Structure
   164â†’
   165â†’### Entity Schema
   166â†’
   167â†’```json
   168â†’{
   169â†’  "name": "PatternName",
   170â†’  "entityType": "Pattern|Solution|Architecture|Tool",
   171â†’  "significance": 8,
   172â†’  "problem": {
   173â†’    "description": "What problem this solves",
   174â†’    "context": "When this problem occurs"
   175â†’  },
   176â†’  "solution": {
   177â†’    "approach": "How to solve it",
   178â†’    "implementation": "Specific implementation details",
   179â†’    "code_example": "Working code snippet"
   180â†’  },
   181â†’  "observations": ["Key insights", "Lessons learned"],
   182â†’  "metadata": {
   183â†’    "technologies": ["React", "Node.js"],
   184â†’    "files": ["src/component.js"],
   185â†’    "references": ["https://docs.example.com"]
   186â†’  }
   187â†’}
   188â†’```
   189â†’
   190â†’### Entity Types
   191â†’
   192â†’- **Pattern**: Reusable solutions and approaches
   193â†’- **Solution**: Specific problem fixes
   194â†’- **Architecture**: System design insights
   195â†’- **Tool**: Technology and framework usage
   196â†’- **Workflow**: Process and methodology insights
   197â†’
   198â†’---
   199â†’
   200â†’## Programmatic API
   201â†’
   202â†’### KnowledgeAPI Class
   203â†’
   204â†’```javascript
   205â†’const { KnowledgeManager } = require('ukb-cli');
   206â†’
   207â†’// Initialize knowledge manager
   208â†’const manager = new KnowledgeManager({
   209â†’  knowledgeBasePath: './knowledge-graph (GraphDB)',
   210â†’  mcpIntegration: true
   211â†’});
   212â†’
   213â†’// Capture structured insight
   214â†’await manager.captureInsight({
   215â†’  name: "ReactHookPattern",
   216â†’  problem: "Stateful logic duplication across components",
   217â†’  solution: "Extract logic into custom hooks",
   218â†’  rationale: "DRY principle and improved testability",
   219â†’  learnings: "Hooks enable better separation of concerns",
   220â†’  applicability: "Any React app with duplicated state logic",
   221â†’  technologies: ["React", "TypeScript"],
   222â†’  references: ["https://reactjs.org/docs/hooks-custom.html"],
   223â†’  significance: 8
   224â†’});
   225â†’
   226â†’// Git analysis
   227â†’const insights = await manager.analyzeGitHistory({
   228â†’  depth: 20,
   229â†’  sinceCommit: 'abc123',
   230â†’  includeCategories: ['feature', 'refactor']
   231â†’});
   232â†’
   233â†’// Search and query
   234â†’const results = await manager.search("authentication pattern");
   235â†’const entities = await manager.getEntitiesByType("TransferablePattern");
   236â†’```
   237â†’
   238â†’---
   239â†’
   240â†’## Common Use Cases
   241â†’
   242â†’### 1. Capturing Bug Fix Patterns
   243â†’
   244â†’**Scenario**: You fixed a tricky bug with React hooks dependency arrays
   245â†’
   246â†’```bash
   247â†’# Interactive capture
   248â†’ukb --interactive
   249â†’
   250â†’? Insight type: Problem-Solution
   251â†’? Problem description: useEffect infinite loop due to object dependency
   252â†’? Solution description: Use useMemo to memoize object dependencies
   253â†’
   254â†’# Quick non-interactive capture
   255â†’ukb entity add -n "ReactHooksDependencyPattern" -t "TechnicalPattern" -s 9 \
   256â†’  -o "Always memoize object and array dependencies in hooks"
   257â†’```
   258â†’
   259â†’### 2. Documenting Architecture Decisions
   260â†’
   261â†’**Scenario**: Team decided to migrate from Redux to Zustand
   262â†’
   263â†’```bash
   264â†’# Create problem entity
   265â†’ukb entity add -n "ReduxComplexityProblem" -t "Problem" -s 7 \
   266â†’  -o "Redux boilerplate becoming unmaintainable with 50+ slices"
   267â†’
   268â†’# Create solution entity
   269â†’ukb entity add -n "ZustandMigrationSolution" -t "Solution" -s 8 \
   270â†’  -o "Migrate to Zustand for simpler state management"
   271â†’
   272â†’# Create relationship
   273â†’ukb relation add -f "ZustandMigrationSolution" -t "ReduxComplexityProblem" \
   274â†’  -r "solves" -s 8
   275â†’```
   276â†’
   277â†’### 3. Post-Mortem Analysis
   278â†’
   279â†’**Scenario**: After production incident, capture learnings
   280â†’
   281â†’```bash
   282â†’# Create incident entity
   283â†’ukb entity add -n "DatabaseConnectionPoolIncident2024" -t "Problem" -s 10 \
   284â†’  -o "Production outage due to connection pool exhaustion"
   285â†’
   286â†’# Add root cause
   287â†’ukb entity add -n "MissingConnectionPoolMonitoring" -t "Problem" -s 9 \
   288â†’  -o "No alerts configured for connection pool usage"
   289â†’
   290â†’# Add solution
   291â†’ukb entity add -n "ConnectionPoolMetricsSolution" -t "Solution" -s 9 \
   292â†’  -o "Implement Prometheus metrics for connection pool monitoring"
   293â†’
   294â†’# Create relationships
   295â†’ukb relation add -f "MissingConnectionPoolMonitoring" \
   296â†’  -t "DatabaseConnectionPoolIncident2024" -r "causes"
   297â†’
   298â†’ukb relation add -f "ConnectionPoolMetricsSolution" \
   299â†’  -t "MissingConnectionPoolMonitoring" -r "solves"
   300â†’```
   301â†’
   302â†’### 4. Onboarding New Team Members
   303â†’
   304â†’**Scenario**: Create knowledge trail for new developers
   305â†’
   306â†’```bash
   307â†’# Export project-specific patterns
   308â†’ukb entity list -t "WorkflowPattern" > onboarding-patterns.txt
   309â†’
   310â†’# Create onboarding checklist
   311â†’ukb entity add -n "NewDeveloperOnboardingChecklist" -t "Documentation" -s 8
   312â†’
   313â†’# Link to key patterns
   314â†’ukb relation add -f "NewDeveloperOnboardingChecklist" \
   315â†’  -t "LocalDevelopmentSetupPattern" -r "references"
   316â†’```
   317â†’
   318â†’---
   319â†’
   320â†’## Domain-Specific Knowledge Bases
   321â†’
   322â†’### Automatic Domain Detection
   323â†’
   324â†’When working in a project directory, UKB automatically creates domain-specific knowledge bases:
   325â†’
   326â†’```bash
   327â†’# Navigate to domain project
   328â†’cd /path/to/raas-project
   329â†’
   330â†’# First ukb command creates domain-specific file
   331â†’ukb --list-entities
   332â†’# Creates: /Users/<username>/Agentic/coding/shared-memory-raas.json
   333â†’
   334â†’# Add domain entity using piped input
   335â†’echo "StreamProcessingPipeline
   336â†’TechnicalPattern
   337â†’8
   338â†’Core pattern for real-time data reprocessing
   339â†’Handles high-throughput data streams with fault tolerance
   340â†’Implemented using Apache Kafka + Apache Flink" | ukb --add-entity
   341â†’```
   342â†’
   343â†’### Cross-Domain Pattern Discovery
   344â†’
   345â†’```bash
   346â†’# Search across all team knowledge bases
   347â†’cd /Users/<username>/Agentic/coding
   348â†’grep -l "MicroserviceArchitecture" team-specific JSON exports
   349â†’
   350â†’# Extract domain-specific implementations
   351â†’ukb --print --team raas | jq '.entities[] | select(.name | contains("Microservice"))'
   352â†’
   353â†’# Create cross-domain pattern in shared knowledge
   354â†’cd /any/project
   355â†’ukb entity add -n "CrossDomainMicroservicePattern" -t "ArchitecturePattern" -s 10 \
   356â†’  -o "Microservice patterns applicable across RaaS and Resilience domains"
   357â†’```
   358â†’
   359â†’---
   360â†’
   361â†’## Migration from Legacy UKB
   362â†’
   363â†’### Automatic Migration
   364â†’
   365â†’All existing `ukb` commands continue to work unchanged. The system automatically delegates to the new Node.js implementation while maintaining full compatibility.
   366â†’
   367â†’#### What Changed
   368â†’
   369â†’- **Internal Architecture**: Bash â†’ Node.js modular design
   370â†’- **Performance**: 3x faster processing, 50% memory reduction
   371â†’- **Features**: Enhanced validation, custom naming, batch operations
   372â†’- **API**: Stable programmatic interface for agent integration
   373â†’
   374â†’#### What Stayed the Same
   375â†’
   376â†’- **Commands**: All existing commands work identically
   377â†’- **Data Format**: knowledge-graph (GraphDB) format unchanged
   378â†’- **Workflows**: Existing team workflows unaffected
   379â†’- **Git Integration**: Same git-based knowledge sharing
   380â†’
   381â†’#### Verification Steps
   382â†’
   383â†’```bash
   384â†’# Verify migration success
   385â†’ukb --validate
   386â†’
   387â†’# Check performance improvement
   388â†’time ukb --list-entities
   389â†’
   390â†’# Test new features
   391â†’ukb --add-entity "TestPattern" --type TransferablePattern
   392â†’ukb --remove-entity "TestPattern"
   393â†’```
   394â†’
   395â†’---
   396â†’
   397â†’## Advanced Features
   398â†’
   399â†’### Batch Operations
   400â†’
   401â†’```bash
   402â†’# Add multiple entities from file
   403â†’ukb --add-multiple-entities entities.json
   404â†’
   405â†’# Import relations from file
   406â†’ukb --import-relations relations.json
   407â†’
   408â†’# Export with filters
   409â†’ukb export --type TechnicalPattern --min-significance 8

309:    const results = [];\\n  > 310:    const visited = new Set(); // Track visited nodes to prevent infinite loops\\n  > 311:    const queue = [{ nodeId: startNodeId, currentDepth: 0, relationshipType: null }];\\n  > 312:\\n  > 313:    // BFS traversal\\n  > 314:    while (queue.length > 0) {\\n  > 315:      const { nodeId, currentDepth, relationshipType } = queue.shift();\\n  > 316:\\n  > 317:      // Skip if we've reached max depth\\n  > 318:      if (currentDepth >= depth) {\\n  > 319:        continue;\\n  > 320:      }\\n  > 321:\\n  > 322:      // Get all neighbors (outbound edges)\\n  > 323:      const neighbors = this.graph.outNeighbors(nodeId);\\n  > 324:\\n  > 325:      for (const neighborId of neighbors) {\\n  > 326:        // Skip if already visited\\n  > 327:        if (visited.has(neighborId)) {\\n  > 328:          continue;\\n  > 329:        }\\n  > 330:\\n  > 331:        // Get edge attributes to find relationship type\\n  > 332:        const edges = this.graph.edges(nodeId, neighborId);\\n  > 333:        const edge = edges[0]; // Get first edge (multi-graph may have multiple)\\n  > 334:        const edgeAttrs = this.graph.getEdgeAttributes(edge);\\n  > 335:        const relType = edgeAttrs.type;\\n  > 336:\\n  > 337:        // Get node attributes\\n  > 338:        const nodeAttrs = this.graph.getNodeAttributes(neighborId);\\n  > 339:\\n  > 340:        // Mark as visited BEFORE filtering\\n  > 341:        visited.add(neighborId);\\n  > 342:\\n  > 343:        // Check if this node matches filters (for inclusion in results)\\n  > 344:        let includeInResults = true;\\n  > 345:\\n  > 346:        // Filter by relationship type\\n  > 347:        if (filter.relationshipType && relType !== filter.relationshipType) {\\n  > 348:          includeInResults = false;\\n  > 349:        }\\n  > 350:\\n  > 351:        // Filter by entity type\\n  > 352:        if (filter.entityType > 357:        if (filter.team && nodeAttrs.team !== filter.team) {\\n  > 358:          includeInResults = false;\\n  > 359:        }\\n  > 360:\\n  > 361:        // Add to results if it matches all filters\\n  > 362:        if (includeInResults) {\\n  > 363:          results.push({\\n  > 364:            entity: nodeAttrs,\\n  > 365:            depth: currentDepth + 1,\\n  > 366:            relationshipType: relType\\n  > 367:          });\\n  > 368:        }\\n  > 369:\\n  > 370:        // Always add to queue for further traversal (to find filtered nodes deeper in the graph)\\n  > 371:        queue.push({\\n  > 372:          nodeId: neighborId,\\n  > 373:          currentDepth: currentDepth + 1,\\n  > 374:          relationshipType: relType\\n  > 375:        });\\n  > 376:      }\\n  > 377:    }\\n  > 378:\\n  > 379:    return results;\\n  > 380:  }\\n  > 381:\\n  > 382:  /**\\n  > 383:   * Query entities with SQL-compatible filtering\\n  > 384:   *\\n  > 385:   * Provides same interface as SQLite <USER_ID_REDACTED> for VKB/UKB compatibility.\\n  > 386:   *\\n  > 387:   * @param {Object} [options={}] - Query options\\n  > 388:   * @param {string} [options.team] - Filter by   } = options;\\n  > 415:\\n  > 416:    // Get all nodes and filter them\\n  > 417:    let results = [];\\n  > 418:    const filteredInsightNodeIds = new Set(); // Only insight nodes (not System, not 536:    });\\n  > 537:\\n  > 538:    // Sort results\\n  > 539:    const validSortFields = ['last_modified', 'extracted_at', 'confidence', 'entity_name'];\\n  > 540:    const safeSortBy = ## Analysis: UKB Documentation vs. Implementation

### Current Architecture (Verified from Code)

**Primary Storage**:
- Graphology in-memory graph database
- LevelDB persistence at `.data/knowledge-graph/`
- Auto-persist every 1000ms

**Secondary Export (Optional)**:
- Team-based JSON files in `.data/knowledge-export/{team}.json`
- Purpose: Backward compatibility with legacy shared-memory format
- Auto-export on entity/relationship changes (debounced 5s)

**No Legacy Files**:
- âŒ No `shared-memory-*.json` files in root directory
- âœ… Migrated to centralized `.data/knowledge-export/`

### Documentation Issues Found

1. **Line 332** - INCORRECT path reference:
   ```
   # Creates: /Users/<username>/Agentic/coding/shared-memory-raas.json
   ```
   Should be: `.data/knowledge-export/raas.json`

2. **Line 209** - Path format unclear:
   ```javascript
   knowledgeBasePath: './knowledge-graph (GraphDB)',
   ```
   Should be: `.data/knowledge-graph`

3. **Missing Architecture Details**:
   - No mention of LevelDB as persistence layer
   - No explanation of export vs. storage distinction
   - No mention that JSON files are optional backward compatibility

File backend: Fast local disk cache (default: .cache/agent-cache/)\\n  >  19: * 2. HTTP backend: Remote cache servers (Redis, Memcached, etc.)\\n  >  20: * 3. MCP backend: MCP Memory server for distributed caching\\n  >  21: */\\n  >  22:\\n  >  23:import fs from 'fs';\\n  >  24:import path from 'path';\\n  >  25:import crypto from 'crypto';\\n  >  26:import { EventEmitter } from 'events';\\n  >  27:\\n  >  28:// Cache entry structure\\n  >  29:class CacheEntry {\\n  >  30:  constructor(key, value, ttl) {\\n  >  31:    this.key = key;\\n  >  32:    this.value = value;\\n  >  33:    this.timestamp = Date.now();\\n  >  34:    this.expiresAt = ttl ? Date.now() + ttl : null;\\n  >  35:    this.hits = 0;\\n  >  36:    this.lastAccessTime = Date.now();\\n  >  37:  }\\n  >  38:\\n  >  39:  isExpired() {\\n  >  40:    return this.expiresAt && Date.now() > this.expiresAt;\\n  >  41:  }\\n  >  42:\\n  >  43:  access() {\\n  >  44:    this.hits++;\\n  >  45:    this.lastAccessTime = Date.now();\\n  >  46:  }\\n  >  47:}\\n  >  48:\\n  >  49:// LRU Cache implementation\\n  >  50:class LRUCache {\\n  >  51:  constructor(maxSize = 1000) {\\n  >  52:    this.maxSize = maxSize;\\n  >  53:    this.cache = new Map(); // key -> CacheEntry\\n  >  54:    this.evictions = 0;\\n  >  55:  }\\n  >  56:\\n  >  57:  get(key) {\\n  >  58:    const entry = this.cache.get(key);\\n  >  59:\\n  >  60:    if (!entry) {\\n  >  61:      return null;\\n  >  62:    }\\n  >  63:\\n  >  64:    if (entry.isExpired()) {\\n  >  65:      this.cache.delete(key);\\n  >  66:      return null;\\n  >  67:    }\\n  >  68:\\n  >  69:    entry.access();\\n  >  70:\\n  >  71:    // Move to end (most recently used)\\n  >  72:    this.cache.delete(key);\\n  >  73:    this.cache.set(key, entry);\\n  >  74:\\n  >  75:    return entry.value;\\n  >  76:  }\\n  >  77:\\n  >  78:  set(key, value, ttl) {\\n  >  79:    // Remove if already exists (to update position)\\n  >  80:    if (this.cache.has(key)) {\\n  >  81:      this.cache.delete(key);\\n  >  82:    }\\n  >  83:\\n  >  84:    // Evict LRU if at capacity\\n  >  85:    if (this.cache.size >= this.maxSize) {\\n  >  86:      const firstKey = this.cache.keys().next().value;\\n  >  87:      this.cache.delete(firstKey);\\n  >  88:      this.evictions++;\\n  >  89:    }\\n  >  90:\\n  >  91:    const entry = new CacheEntry(key, value, ttl);\\n  >  92:    this.cache.set(key, entry);\\n  >  93:  }\\n  >  94:\\n  >  95:  delete(key) {\\n  >  96:    return this.cache.delete(key);\\n  >  97:  }\\n  >  98:\\n  >  99:  clear() {\\n  > 100:    this.cache.clear();\\n  > 101:  }\\n  > 102:\\n  > 103:  size() {\\n  > 104:    return this.cache.size;\\n  > 105:  }\\n  > 106:\\n  > 107:  getStats() {\\n  > 108:    let totalHits = 0;\\n  > 109:    let oldestAccess = Date.now();\\n  > 110:    let newestAccess = 0;\\n  > 111:\\n  > 112:    for (const entry of this.cache.values()) {\\n  > 113:      totalHits += entry.hits;\\n  > 114:      if (entry.lastAccessTime < oldestAccess) oldestAccess = entry.lastAccessTime;\\n  > 115:      if (entry.lastAccessTime > newestAccess) newestAccess = entry.lastAccessTime;\\n  > 116:    }\\n  > 117:\\n  > 118:    return {\\n  > 119:      size: this.cache.size,\\n  > 120:      maxSize: this.maxSize,\\n  > 121:      evictions: this.evictions,\\n  > 122:      totalHits,\\n  > 123:      averageHits: this.cache.size > 0 ? totalHits / this.cache.size : 0,\\n  > 124:      oldestAccess,\\n  > 125:      newestAccess\\n  > 126:    };\\n  > 127:  }\\n  > 128:}\\n  > 129:\\n  > 130:// File backend for local disk caching\\n  > 131:class FileBackend {\\n  > 132:  constructor(config = {}) {\\n  > 133:    this.cacheDir = config.cacheDir || path.join(process.cwd(), '.cache', 'agent-cache');\\n  > 134:    this.enabled = config.enabled !== false;\\n  > 135:\\n  > 136:    // Create cache directory if it doesn't exist\\n  > 137:    if (this.enabled && !fs.existsSync(this.cacheDir)) {\\n  > 138:      fs.mkdirSync(this.cacheDir, { recursive: true });\\n  > 139:    }\\n  > 140:  }\\n  > 141:\\n  > 142:  async get(key) {\\n  > 143:    if (!this.enabled) return null;\\n  > 144:\\n  > 145:    try {\\n  > 146:      const filePath = this.getFilePath(key);\\n  > 147:\\n  > 148:      if (!fs.existsSync(filePath)) {\\n  > 149:        return null;\\n  > 150:      }\\n  > 151:\\n  > 152:      const data = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8'));\\n  > 153:\\n  > 154:      // Check expiration\\n  > 155:      if (data.expiresAt && Date.now() > data.expiresAt) {\\n  > 156:        fs.unlinkSync(filePath);\\n  > 157:        return null;\\n  > 158:      }\\n  > 159:\\n  > 160:      return data.value;\\n  > 161:    } catch (error) {\\n  > 162:      console.warn('[FileBackend] Get error:', error);\\n  > 163:      return null;\\n  > 164:    }\\n  > 165:  }\\n  > 166:\\n  > 167:  async set(key, value, ttl) {\\n  > 168:    if (!this.enabled) return false;\\n  > 169:\\n  > 170:    try {\\n  > 171:      const filePath = this.getFilePath(key);\\n  > 172:      const data = {\\n  > 173:        key,\\n  > 174:        value,\\n  > 175:        timestamp: Date.now(),\\n  > 176:        expiresAt: ttl ? Date.now() + ttl : null\\n  > 177:      };\\n  > 178:\\n  > 179:      fs.writeFileSync(filePath, JSON.stringify(data, null, 2), 'utf-8');\\n  > 180:      return true;\\n  > 181:    } catch (error) {\\n  > 182:      console.warn('[FileBackend] Set error:', error);\\n  > 183:      return false;\\n  > 184:    }\\n  > 185:  }\\n  > 186:\\n  > 187:  async delete(key) {\\n  > 188:    if (!this.enabled) return false;\\n  > 189:\\n  > 190:    try {\\n  > 191:      const filePath = this.getFilePath(key);\\n  > 192:      if (fs.existsSync(filePath)) {\\n  > 193:        fs.unlinkSync(filePath);\\n  > 194:        return true;\\n  > 195:      }\\n  > 196:      return false;\\n  > 197:    } catch (error) {\\n  > 198:      console.warn('[FileBackend] Delete error:', error);\\n  > 199:      return false;\\n  > 200:    }\\n  > 201:  }\\n  > 202:\\n  > 203:  async clear() {\\n  > 204:    if (!this.enabled) return false;\\n  > 205:\\n  > 206:    try {\\n  > 207:      const files = fs.readdirSync(this.cacheDir);\\n  > 208:      for (const file of files) {\\n  > 209:        fs.unlinkSync(path.join(this.cacheDir, file));\\n  > 210:      }\\n  > 211:      return true;\\n  > 212:    } catch (error) {\\n  > 213:      console.warn('[FileBackend] Clear error:', error);\\n  > 214:      return false;\\n  > 215:    }\\n  > 216:  }\\n  > 217:\\n  > 218:  getFilePath(key) {\\n  > 219:    const hash = crypto.createHash('sha256').update(key).digest('hex');\\n  > 220:    return path.join(this.cacheDir, `${hash}.json`);\\n  > 221:  }\\n  > 222:\\n  > 223:  getStats() {\\n  > 224:    if (!this.enabled) {\\n  > 225:      return { enabled: false };\\n  > 226:    }\\n  > 227:\\n  > 228:    try {\\n  > 229:      const files = fs.readdirSync(this.cacheDir);\\n  > 230:      let totalSize = 0;\\n  > 231:\\n  > 232:      for (const file of files) {\\n  > 233:        const stats = fs.statSync(path.join(this.cacheDir, file));\\n  > 234:        totalSize += stats.size;\\n  > 235:      }\\n  > 236:\\n  > 237:      return {\\n  > 238:        enabled: true,\\n  > 239:        entries: files.length,\\n  > 240:        totalSize,\\n  > 241:        cacheDir: this.cacheDir\\n  > 242:      };\\n  > 243:    } catch (error) {\\n  > 244:      return { enabled: true, error: error.message };\\n  > 245:    }\\n  > 246:  }\\n  > 247:}\\n  > 248:\\n  > 249:// HTTP backend for Redis/Memcached/etc\\n  > 250:class HTTPBackend {\\n  > 251:  constructor(config = {}) {\\n  > 252:    this.baseUrl = config.baseUrl; // e.g., http://localhost:6379\\n  > 253:    this.enabled = config.enabled && !!this.baseUrl;\\n  > 254:    this.timeout = config.timeout || 5000;\\n  > 255:  }\\n  > 256:\\n  > 257:  async get(key) {\\n  > 258:    if (!this.enabled) return null;\\n  > 259:\\n  > 260:    try {\\n  > 261:      const response = await fetch(`${this.baseUrl}/get/${encodeURIComponent(key)}`, {\\n  > 262:        signal: AbortSignal.timeout(this.timeout)\\n  > 263:      });\\n  > 264:\\n  > 265:      if (!response.ok) {\\n  > 266:        return null;\\n  > 267:      }\\n  > 268:\\n  > 269:      const data = await response.json();\\n  > 270:      return data.value;\\n  > 271:    } catch (error) {\\n  > 272:      console.warn('[HTTPBackend] Get error:', error.message);\\n  > 273:      return null;\\n  > 274:    }\\n  > 275:  }\\n  > 276:\\n  > 277:  async set(key, value, ttl) {\\n  > 278:    if (!this.enabled) return false;\\n  > 279:\\n  > 280:    try {\\n  > 281:      const response = await fetch(`${this.baseUrl}/set`, {\\n  > 282:        method: 'POST',\\n  > 283:        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\\n  > 284:        body: JSON.stringify({ key, value, ttl }),\\n  > 285:        signal: AbortSignal.timeout(this.timeout)\\n  > 286:      });\\n  > 287:\\n  > 288:      return response.ok;\\n  > 289:    } catch (error) {\\n  > 290:      console.warn('[HTTPBackend] Set error:', error.message);\\n  > 291:      return false;\\n  > 292:    }\\n  > 293:  }\\n  > 294:\\n  > 295:  async delete(key) {\\n  > 296:    if (!this.enabled) return false;\\n  > 297:\\n  > 298:    try {\\n  > 299:      const response = await fetch(`${this.baseUrl}/delete/${encodeURIComponent(key)}`, {\\n  > 300:        method: 'DELETE',\\n  > 301:        signal: AbortSignal.timeout(this.timeout)\\n  > 302:      });\\n  > 303:\\n  > 304:      return response.ok;\\n  > 305:    } catch (error) {\\n  > 306:      console.warn('[HTTPBackend] Delete error:', error.message);\\n  > 307:      return false;\\n  > 308:    }\\n  > 309:  }\\n  > 310:\\n  > 311:  async clear() {\\n  > 312:    if (!this.enabled) return false;\\n  > 313:\\n  > 314:    try {\\n  > 315:      const response = await fetch(`${this.baseUrl}/clear`, {\\n  > 316:        method: 'POST',\\n  > 317:        signal: AbortSignal.timeout(this.timeout)\\n  > 318:      });\\n  > 319:\\n  > 320:      return response.ok;\\n  > 321:    } catch (error) {\\n  > 322:      console.warn('[HTTPBackend] Clear error:', error.message);\\n  > 323:      return false;\\n  > 324:    }\\n  > 325:  }\\n  > 326:\\n  > 327:  getStats() {\\n  > 328:    return {\\n  > 329:      enabled: this.enabled,\\n  > 330:      baseUrl: this.baseUrl\\n  > 331:    };\\n  > 332:  }\\n  > 333:}\\n  > 334:\\n  > 335:// MCP backend for MCP Memory server\\n  > 336:class MCPBackend {\\n  > 337:  constructor(config = {}) {\\n  > 338:    this.enabled = config.enabled || false;\\n  > 339:    this.serverName = config.serverName || 'memory';\\n  > 340:  }\\n  > 341:\\n  > 342:  async get(key) {\\n  > 343:    if (!this.enabled) return null;\\n  > 344:\\n  > 345:    try {\\n  > 346:      // Search for entity with this cache key\\n  > 347:      const result = await this.mcpCall('search_nodes', { query: key });\\n  > 348:\\n  > 349:      if (!result || !result.entities || result.entities.length === 0) {\\n  > 350:        return null;\\n  > 351:      }\\n  > 352:\\n  > 353:      // Find matching entity\\n  > 354:      const entity = result.entities.find(e => e.name === key);\\n  > 355:      if (!entity) return null;\\n  > 356:\\n  > 357:      // Parse value from observations\\n  > 358:      const valueObs = entity.observations.find(o => o.startsWith('value:'));\\n  > 359:      if (!valueObs) return null;\\n  > 360:\\n  > 361:      const value = JSON.parse(valueObs.substring(6));\\n  > 362:\\n  > 363:      // Check expiration\\n  > 364:      const expiresObs = entity.observations.find(o => o.startsWith('expiresAt:'));\\n  > 365:      if (expiresObs) {\\n  > 366:        const expiresAt = parseInt(expiresObs.substring(10));\\n  > 367:        if (Date.now() > expiresAt) {\\n  > 368:          await this.delete(key);\\n  > 369:          return null;\\n  > 370:        }\\n  > 371:      }\\n  > 372:\\n  > 373:      return value;\\n  > 374:    } catch (error) {\\n  > 375:      console.warn('[MCPBackend] Get error:', error.message);\\n  > 376:      return null;\\n  > 377:    }\\n  > 378:  }\\n  > 379:\\n  > 380:  async set(key, value, ttl) {\\n  > 381:    if (!this.enabled) return false;\\n  > 382:\\n  > 383:    try {\\n  > 384:      const observations = [\\n  > 385:        `value:${JSON.stringify(value)}`,\\n  > 386:        `timestamp:${Date.now()}`\\n  > 387:      ];\\n  > 388:\\n  > 389:      if (ttl) {\\n  > 390:        observations.push(`expiresAt:${Date.now() + ttl}`);\\n  > 391:      }\\n  > 392:\\n  > 393:      await this.mcpCall('create_entities', {\\n  > 394:        entities: [{\\n  > 395:          name: key,\\n  > 396:          entityType: 'cache-entry',\\n  > 397:          observations\\n  > 398:        }]\\n  > 399:      });\\n  > 400:\\n  > 401:      return true;\\n  > 402:    } catch (error) {\\n  > 403:      console.warn('[MCPBackend] Set error:', error.message);\\n  > 404:      return false;\\n  > 405:    }\\n  > 406:  }\\n  > 407:\\n  > 408:  async delete(key) {\\n  > 409:    if (!this.enabled) return false;\\n  > 410:\\n  > 411:    try {\\n  > 412:      await this.mcpCall('delete_entities', {\\n  > 413:        entityNames: [key]\\n  > 414:      });\\n  > 415:      return true;\\n  > 416:    } catch (error) {\\n  > 417:      console.warn('[MCPBackend] Delete error:', error.message);\\n  > 418:      return false;\\n  > 419:    }\\n  > 420:  }\\n  > 421:\\n  > 422:  async clear() {\\n  > 423:    if (!this.enabled) return false;\\n  > 424:\\n  > 425:    try {\\n  > 426:      // Get all cache entities\\n  > 427:      const result = await this.mcpCall('search_nodes', { query: 'cache-entry' });\\n  > 428:\\n  > 429:      if (result && result.entities && result.entities.length > 0) {\\n  > 430:        const entityNames = result.entities\\n  > 431:          .filter(e => e.type === 'cache-entry')\\n  > 432:          .map(e => e.name);\\n  > 433:\\n  > 434:        if (entityNames.length > 0) {\\n  > 435:          await this.mcpCall('delete_entities', { entityNames });\\n  > 436:        }\\n  > 437:      }\\n  > 438:\\n  > 439:      return true;\\n  > 440:    } catch (error) {\\n  > 441:      console.warn('[MCPBackend] Clear error:', error.message);\\n  > 442:      return false;\\n  > 443:    }\\n  > 444:  }\\n  > 445:\\n  > 446:  async mcpCall(method, params) {\\n  > 447:    // Placeholder for MCP call - will be replaced with actual MCP client\\n  > 448:    // This would use the MCP protocol to communicate with the memory server\\n  > 449:    throw new Error('MCP backend not yet implemented - requires MCP client integration');\\n  > 450:  }\\n  > 451:\\n  > 452:  getStats() {\\n  > 453:    return {\\n  > 454:      enabled: this.enabled,\\n  > 455:      serverName: this.serverName\\n  > 456:    };\\n  > 457:  }\\n  > 458:}\\n  > 459:\\n  > 460:export class AgentAgnosticCache extends EventEmitter {\\n  > 461:  constructor(config = {}) {\\n  > 462:    super();\\n  > 463:\\n  > 464:    this.config = config;\\n  > 465:\\n  > 466:    // LRU cache for in-memory caching\\n  > 467:    this.lruCache = new LRUCache(config.maxSize || 1000);\\n  > 468:\\n  > 469:    // Default TTL (1 hour)\\n  > 470:    this.defaultTTL = config.defaultTTL || 60 * 60 * 1000;\\n  > 471:\\n  > 472:    // Backend configuration\\n  > 473:    this.backends = {\\n  > 474:      file: new FileBackend(config.file || {}),\\n  > 475:      http: new HTTPBackend(config.http || {}),\\n  > 476:      mcp: new MCPBackend(config.mcp || {})\\n  > 477:    };\\n  > 478:\\n  > 479:    // Backend priority (try in this order)\\n  > 480:    this.backendPriority = config.backendPriority || ['file', 'http', 'mcp'];\\n  > 481:\\n  > 482:    // Statistics\\n  > 483:    this.stats = {\\n  > 484:      hits: 0,\\n  > 485:      misses: 0,\\n  > 486:      sets: 0,\\n  > 487:      deletes: 0,\\n  > 488:      errors: 0,\\n  > 489:      byBackend: {\\n  > 490:        memory: { hits: 0, misses: 0, sets: 0, errors: 0 },\\n  > 491:        file: { hits: 0, misses: 0, sets: 0, errors: 0 },\\n  > 492:        http: { hits: 0, misses: 0, sets: 0, errors: 0 },\\n  > 493:        mcp: { hits: 0, misses: 0, sets: 0, errors: 0 }\\n  > 494:      }\\n  > 495:    };\\n  > 496:\\n  > 497:    console.log('[AgentAgnosticCache] Initialized with backends:', this.backendPriority.join(', '));\\n  > 498:  }\\n  > 499:\\n  > 500:  /**\\n  > 501:   * Generate cache key from input\\n  > 502:   */\\n  > 503:  generateKey(input, namespace = 'default') {\\n  > 504:    const normalized = typeof input === 'string' ? input : JSON.stringify(input);\\n  > 505:    const hash = crypto.createHash('sha256').update(normalized).digest('hex');\\n  > 506:    return `${namespace}:${hash}`;\\n  > 507:  }\\n  > 508:\\n  > 509:  /**\\n  > 510:   * Get value from cache\\n  > 511:   * Tries memory first, then backends in priority order\\n  > 512:   */\\n  > 513:  async get(key) {\\n  > 514:    const startTime = Date.now();\\n  > 515:\\n  > 516:    try {\\n  > 517:      // 1. Try in-memory LRU cache first\\n  > 518:      const memoryValue = this.lruCache.get(key);\\n  > 519:      if (memoryValue !== null) {\\n  > 520:        this.stats.hits++;\\n  > 521:        this.stats.byBackend.memory.hits++;\\n  > 522:        this.emit('cache-hit', { key, backend: 'memory', duration: Date.now() - startTime });\\n  > 523:        return memoryValue;\\n  > 524:      }\\n  > 525:\\n  > 526:      this.stats.byBackend.memory.misses++;\\n  > 527:\\n  > 528:      // 2. Try backends in priority order\\n  > 529:      for (const backendName of this.backendPriority) {\\n  > 530:        const backend = this.backends[backendName];\\n  > 531:\\n  > 532:        if (!backend.enabled) {\\n  > 533:          continue;\\n  > 534:        }\\n  > 535:\\n  > 536:        try {\\n  > 537:          const value = await backend.get(key);\\n  > 538:\\n  > 539:          if (value !== null) {\\n  > 540:            // Cache hit - store in memory for faster access\\n  > 541:            this.lruCache.set(key, value, this.defaultTTL);\\n  > 542:\\n  > 543:            this.stats.hits++;\\n  > 544:            this.stats.byBackend[backendName].hits++;\\n  > 545:            this.emit('cache-hit', { key, backend: backendName, duration: Date.now() - startTime });\\n  > 546:\\n  > 547:            return value;\\n  > 548:          }\\n  > 549:\\n  > 550:          this.stats.byBackend[backendName].misses++;\\n  > 551:        } catch (error) {\\n  > 552:          this.stats.byBackend[backendName].errors++;\\n  > 553:          console.warn(`[AgentAgnosticCache] ${backendName} backend error:`, error);\\n  > 554:          continue; // Try next backend\\n  > 555:        }\\n  > 556:      }\\n  > 557:\\n  > 558:      // Cache miss\\n  > 559:      this.stats.misses++;\\n  > 560:      this.emit('cache-miss', { key, duration: Date.now() - startTime });\\n  > 561:\\n  > 562:      return null;\\n  > 563:\\n  > 564:    } catch (error) {\\n  > 565:      this.stats.errors++;\\n  > 566:      console.error('[AgentAgnosticCache] Get error:', error);\\n  > 567:      return null;\\n  > 568:    }\\n  > 569:  }\\n  > 570:\\n  > 571:  /**\\n  > 572:   * Set value in cache\\n  > 573:   * Writes to memory and all enabled backends\\n  > 574:   */\\n  > 575:  async set(key, value, ttl = null) {\\n  > 576:    const startTime = Date.now();\\n  > 577:    const effectiveTTL = ttl || this.defaultTTL;\\n  > 578:\\n  > 579:    try {\\n  > 580:      // 1. Store in memory\\n  > 581:      this.lruCache.set(key, value, effectiveTTL);\\n  > 582:      this.stats.byBackend.memory.sets++;\\n  > 583:\\n  > 584:      // 2. Store in all enabled backends (fire and forget)\\n  > 585:      const backendPromises = [];\\n  > 586:\\n  > 587:      for (const backendName of this.backendPriority) {\\n  > 588:        const backend = this.backends[backendName];\\n  > 589:\\n  > 590:        if (!backend.enabled) {\\n  > 591:          continue;\\n  > 592:        }\\n  > 593:\\n  > 594:        backendPromises.push(\\n  > 595:          backend.set(key, value, effectiveTTL)\\n  > 596:            .then(success => {\\n  > 597:              if (success) {\\n  > 598:                this.stats.byBackend[backendName].sets++;\\n  > 599:              } else {\\n  > 600:                this.stats.byBackend[backendName].errors++;\\n  > 601:              }\\n  > 602:              return success;\\n  > 603:            })\\n  > 604:            .catch(error => {\\n  > 605:              this.stats.byBackend[backendName].errors++;\\n  > 606:              console.warn(`[AgentAgnosticCache] ${backendName} set error:`, error);\\n  > 607:              return false;\\n  > 608:            })\\n  > 609:        );\\n  > 610:      }\\n  > 611:\\n  > 612:      // Wait for all backends (but don't fail if some fail)\\n  > 613:      await Promise.allSettled(backendPromises);\\n  > 614:\\n  > 615:      this.stats.sets++;\\n  > 616:      this.emit('cache-set', { key, ttl: effectiveTTL, duration: Date.now() - startTime });\\n  > 617:\\n  > 618:      return true;\\n  > 619:    } catch (error) {\\n  > 620:      this.stats.errors++;\\n  > 621:      console.error('[AgentAgnosticCache] Set error:', error);\\n  > 622:      return false;\\n  > 623:    }\\n  > 624:  }\\n  > 625:\\n  > 626:  /**\\n  > 627:   * Delete value from cache\\n  > 628:   * Removes from memory and all backends\\n  > 629:   */\\n  > 630:  async delete(key) {\\n  > 631:    try {\\n  > 632:      // 1. Delete from memory\\n  > 633:      this.lruCache.delete(key);\\n  > 634:\\n  > 635:      // 2. Delete from all backends\\n  > 636:      const backendPromises = [];\\n  > 637:\\n  > 638:      for (const backendName of this.backendPriority) {\\n  > 639:        const backend = this.backends[backendName];\\n  > 640:\\n  > 641:        if (!backend.enabled) {\\n  > 642:          continue;\\n  > 643:        }\\n  > 644:\\n  > 645:        backendPromises.push(\\n  > 646:          backend.delete(key).catch(error => {\\n  > 647:            console.warn(`[AgentAgnosticCache] ${backendName} delete error:`, error);\\n  > 648:            return false;\\n  > 649:          })\\n  > 650:        );\\n  > 651:      }\\n  > 652:\\n  > 653:      await Promise.allSettled(backendPromises);\\n  > 654:\\n  > 655:      this.stats.deletes++;\\n  > 656:      this.emit('cache-delete', { key });\\n  > 657:\\n  > 658:      return true;\\n  > 659:    } catch (error) {\\n  > 660:      this.stats.errors++;\\n  > 661:      console.error('[AgentAgnosticCache] Delete error:', error);\\n  > 662:      return false;\\n  > 663:    }\\n  > 664:  }\\n  > 665:\\n  > 666:  /**\\n  > 667:   * Clear all cache entries\\n  > 668:   */\\n  > 669:  async clear() {\\n  > 670:    try {\\n  > 671:      // 1. Clear memory\\n  > 672:      this.lruCache.clear();\\n  > 673:\\n  > 674:      // 2. Clear all backends\\n  > 675:      const backendPromises = [];\\n  > 676:\\n  > 677:      for (const backendName of this.backendPriority) {\\n  > 678:        const backend = this.backends[backendName];\\n  > 679:\\n  > 680:        if (!backend.enabled) {\\n  > 681:          continue;\\n  > 682:        }\\n  > 683:\\n  > 684:        backendPromises.push(\\n  > 685:          backend.clear().catch(error => {\\n  > 686:            console.warn(`[AgentAgnosticCache] ${backendName} clear error:`, error);\\n  > 687:            return false;\\n  > 688:          })\\n  > 689:        );\\n  > 690:      }\\n  > 691:\\n  > 692:      await Promise.allSettled(backendPromises);\\n  > 693:\\n  > 694:      this.emit('cache-clear');\\n  > 695:\\n  > 696:      return true;\\n  > 697:    } catch (error) {\\n  > 698:      this.stats.errors++;\\n  > 699:      console.error('[AgentAgnosticCache] Clear error:', error);\\n  > 700:      return false;\\n  > 701:    }\\n  > 702:  }\\n  > 703:\\n  > 704:  /**\\n  > 705:   * Get cache statistics\\n  > 706:   */\\n  > 707:  getStats() {\\n  > 708:    const lruStats = this.lruCache.getStats();\\n  > 709:    const hitRate = this.stats.hits + this.stats.misses > 0\\n  > 710:      ? (this.stats.hits / (this.stats.hits + this.stats.misses)) * 100\\n  > 711:      : 0;\\n  > 712:\\n  > 713:    return {\\n  > 714:      hits: this.stats.hits,\\n  > 715:      misses: this.stats.misses,\\n  > 716:      sets: this.stats.sets,\\n  > 717:      deletes: this.stats.deletes,\\n  > 718:      errors: this.stats.errors,\\n  > 719:      hitRate: hitRate.toFixed(2) + '%',\\n  > 720:      lru: lruStats,\\n  > 721:      byBackend: this.stats.byBackend,\\n  > 722:      backends: {\\n  > 723:        file: this.backends.file.getStats(),\\n  > 724:        http: this.backends.http.getStats(),\\n  > 725:        mcp: this.backends.mcp.getStats()\"]}"}

## 2. Key Technical Concepts

- **GraphDB + LevelDB Architecture**: Primary storage using Graphology in-memory graph with LevelDB persistence
- **DatabaseManager**: Orchestrates SQLite, GraphDB, and optional Qdrant vector DB
- **UKBDatabaseWriter**: Writes knowledge entities and relations to database
- **GraphDatabaseService**: Manages Graphology graph and LevelDB persistence with auto-persist (1000ms)
- **GraphKnowledgeExporter**: Optional JSON export for backward compatibility (debounced 5000ms)
- **Ontology Integration**: StreamingKnowledgeExtractor uses OntologyClassifier for entity classification
- **Semantic Analysis MCP**: Integration with mcp-server-semantic-analysis for significance determination
- **Constraint System**: Real-time code <USER_ID_REDACTED> enforcement via PreToolUse hooks
- **JSON Export vs Storage**: `.data/knowledge-export/{team}.json` are exports, NOT primary storage
- **Deprecated**: MCP Memory Server (removed), shared-memory-*.json files in root (migrated)

### UKB Implementation Files (Examined via Serena)

**`lib/ukb-database/cli.js`**
- Entry point for UKB CLI
- Functions: `initializeDatabase`, `displayStatus`, `addEntityFromStdin`, `addRelationFromStdin`, `importBatch`, `exportToJson`
- Delegates to DatabaseManager and UKBDatabaseWriter

**`src/databases/DatabaseManager.js`**  
- Orchestrates multiple database backends
- Methods: `initializeGraphDB`, `initializeSQLite`, `initializeQdrant`
- Manages health status for all database systems

**`src/knowledge-management/GraphDatabaseService.js`**
- Core graph database implementation
- Uses Graphology (in-memory) + LevelDB (persistence)
- Methods: `storeEntity`, `storeRelationship`, `queryEntities`, `queryByOntologyClass`, `exportToJSON`
- Auto-persist mechanism with 1000ms interval
- Fail-fast semantics on database errors

**`src/knowledge-management/UKBDatabaseWriter.js`**
- Writes entities and relations to database
- Methods: `storeEntity`, `storeRelation`, `exportToJson`, `generateAndStoreEmbedding`
- Integrates with DatabaseManager for persistence

**`src/knowledge-management/StreamingKnowledgeExtractor.js`**
- **ONTOLOGY INTEGRATION FOUND**: Lines 403-448
```javascript
if (this.ontologyEnabled && this.ontologyClassifier) {
  const ontologyClassification = await this.ontologyClassifier.classify(
    knowledgeItem,
    {
      team: this.ontologyConfig.team,
      minConfidence: this.ontologyConfig.confidenceThreshold || 0.7,
      useHeuristics: this.ontologyConfig.classification?.useHeuristicFallback !== false,
      useLLM: this.ontologyConfig.classification?.enableLayer4 !== false
    }
  );
  
  if (ontologyClassification) {
    knowledgeItem.ontology = {
      entityClass: ontologyClassification.entityClass,
      confidence: ontologyClassification.confidence,
      team: ontologyClassification.team,
      method: ontologyClassification.method,
      layer: ontologyClassification.layer,
      properties: ontologyClassification.properties || {}
    };
  }
}
```

**`src/knowledge-management/KnowledgeRetriever.js`**
- Includes ontology-based retrieval: `getByOntologyClass` method
- Integrates with OntologyQueryEngine

**Fix**: Removed content-based triggers (`Architecture`, `## Architecture`) from pattern:
```yaml
# Before:
pattern: "(?:```(?:plantuml|puml|mermaid)|@startuml|flowchart|sequenceDiagram|Architecture|## Architecture)"
# After:
pattern: "(?:```(?:plantuml|puml|mermaid)|@startuml|flowchart|sequenceDiagram)"
```

### Error 3: Session ID Mismatch for Constraint Override
**Problem**: Override state file used different session ID (PPID vs CLAUDE_SESSION_ID)
**Context**: User asked to use constraint override mechanism but it wasn't working
**Fix**: Identified the session ID resolution logic in `prompt-override-parser.js` - uses `CLAUDE_SESSION_ID` || `process.ppid` || `Date.now()`
**Outcome**: Documented the override mechanism instead of relying on it for this session

## Prompt Set 7 (ps_1763287022589)

**Time:** 2025-11-16T09:57:02.589Z

### User

Base directory for this skill: /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/.claude/skills/documentation-style

# Documentation Styling Rules

This skill enforces comprehensive documentation standards across all projects.

## Critical Rules

### 1. NO LINE ART - EVER
**ABSOLUTE RULE**: Never create ASCII art or line-based diagrams in documentation.

**ALWAYS USE**:
- PlantUML for architecture diagrams, sequence diagrams, component diagrams
- Mermaid for flowcharts, state diagrams, simple visualizations

**WHY**: Text-based "line art" is not accessible, difficult to maintain, and looks unprofessional.

### 2. PlantUML Diagram Standards

**Location**: All PlantUML files MUST be stored in `docs/puml/`

**Style Sheet**: ALWAYS include the standard style sheet from coding project as the FIRST line after the opening tag.

**Layout Guidelines**:
- **Standard diagrams**: Prefer VERTICAL layouts to avoid excessive width
- Reason: Prevents users from zooming and scrolling horizontally
- Vertical scrolling is acceptable and preferred over horizontal scrolling
- Aim for narrow, tall diagrams that fit within typical screen widths

**Workflow for Creating PlantUML Diagrams**:

1. **Create the .puml file** in `docs/puml/` with proper naming
2. **Include standard style** - see reference documentation for the exact include syntax
3. **Design with vertical layout** - stack components top-to-bottom when possible
4. **Validate syntax** by attempting to render with plantuml checkonly flag
5. **Fix any errors** reported by plantuml validation
6. **Generate PNG** once error-free using plantuml command
7. **Move PNG to images folder** in docs/images/
8. **Reference in markdown** using relative path to the image

**IMPORTANT**: Never claim success until you've verified the PNG was created without errors.

### 3. Filename Conventions

**STRICT RULES** for ALL documentation artifacts (`.md`, `.puml`, `.png`, etc.):

**Permitted characters**:
- Lowercase letters: `a-z`
- Hyphens: `-`
- Numbers: `0-9`
- Extensions: `.md`, `.puml`, `.png`, etc.

**ONLY permitted exception**: `README.md` (capital letters allowed)

**Good Examples**:
- `system-architecture.puml`
- `deployment-flow.md`
- `api-endpoints.png`
- `README.md` (exception)

**Bad Examples**:
- Capital letters in names
- Underscores instead of hyphens
- CamelCase or PascalCase naming

### 4. NO INCREMENTAL NAMING

**CRITICAL**: Filenames and diagram text MUST represent the CURRENT STATE only, never showing evolution.

**FORBIDDEN PATTERNS** - Never use these suffixes or words:
- Version numbers or indicators
- Words suggesting improvement or change
- Words suggesting temporary status
- Words suggesting alternatives

**Why**: Documentation should reflect current state, not history. Use git for version history.

**Always**: Update the original file directly instead of creating variants.

### 5. Diagram Text Content

Text WITHIN diagrams must also be non-incremental:
- Component names should be simple and current
- Node labels should not indicate versions
- Actor names should not suggest enhancement status

## Implementation Checklist

When creating or updating documentation, verify:

- [ ] No ASCII/line art used (use PlantUML or Mermaid)
- [ ] PlantUML files stored in `docs/puml/`
- [ ] Standard style sheet included in .puml files
- [ ] PlantUML syntax validated with plantuml checkonly
- [ ] PNG generated successfully with plantuml
- [ ] PNG moved to `docs/images/`
- [ ] All filenames use lowercase + hyphens only (except README.md)
- [ ] No incremental suffixes in filenames
- [ ] No incremental labels in diagram text
- [ ] Markdown properly references images from `docs/images/`

## Tool Requirements

**Required tool**: `plantuml` must be installed on the system.

**Verification**:
```bash
which plantuml || echo "ERROR: plantuml not installed"
```

## Error Recovery

If PlantUML generation fails:

1. **Read the error message carefully** - PlantUML errors are usually specific
2. **Check syntax** - common issues include missing tags, unclosed quotes, invalid stereotypes, incorrect arrow syntax
3. **Validate include path** - ensure style sheet path is correct
4. **Test incrementally** - comment out sections to isolate problems

## Project-Specific Paths

### Standard Mode Style Sheet
Located at: `/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/docs/puml/_standard-style.puml`

Use this path for regular documentation diagrams (12pt fonts, 2pt lines, vertical layout preference).

### Presentation Mode Style Sheet
Located at: `/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/docs/presentation/puml/_standard-style.puml`

Use this path for presentation diagrams (18pt fonts, 3-4pt lines, horizontal layout preference).

**IMPORTANT**: Both style sheets are named `_standard-style.puml` but are in different directories. The constraint monitor requires all PlantUML files to include a file named `_standard-style.puml`, so we use the same name in both locations but with different content optimized for each use case.

## PRESENTATION MODE

### When to Use Presentation Mode

Create a presentation mode version when:
- User explicitly requests "presentation mode" or "PPT version"
- Diagram will be used in PowerPoint or similar presentation software
- Diagram needs to be readable from distance (projector/large screen)
- Focus should be on key concepts, not detailed annotations

### Presentation Mode Workflow

When asked to create a presentation mode version:

1. **Copy source file** from `docs/puml/` to `coding/docs/presentation/puml/`
   - Keep the same filename (no suffix changes)
   - This is stored in coding project for reuse across all projects

2. **Rework the diagram** with these changes:
   - **Thicker lines**: All connections and borders become more prominent
   - **Increased font size**: All text becomes larger (18pt vs 12pt)
   - **Essential text only**: Remove verbose labels, keep only critical identifiers
   - **Remove annotations**: Delete all notes, legends, and explanatory text
   - **Horizontal layout**: Arrange for landscape PPT slide (left-to-right flow)
   - **Simplify**: Focus on core concepts, remove implementation details

3. **Update style sheet include** to presentation style:

   **Absolute path** (when referencing from any project):
   ```
   !include /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/docs/presentation/puml/_standard-style.puml
   ```

   **Relative path** (when file is in the presentation/puml directory):
   ```
   !include _standard-style.puml
   ```

   Note: This is a different `_standard-style.puml` than the regular one - it's the presentation mode version with larger fonts and thicker lines.

4. **Validate and generate**:
   ```bash
   plantuml -checkonly coding/docs/presentation/puml/diagram-name.puml
   plantuml coding/docs/presentation/puml/diagram-name.puml
   mv coding/docs/presentation/puml/diagram-name.png coding/docs/presentation/images/
   ```

5. **Verify** the presentation PNG is created and suitable for PPT use

### Presentation Mode Characteristics

**Differences from Standard Mode**:

| Aspect | Standard Mode | Presentation Mode |
|--------|--------------|-------------------|
| Layout | Vertical (narrow, tall) | Horizontal (wide, landscape) |
| Font Size | 12pt | 18pt |
| Line Thickness | 2pt | 3-4pt |
| Text Detail | Comprehensive | Essential only |
| Annotations | Included | Removed |
| Notes/Legends | Present | Omitted |
| Purpose | Documentation | Presentation |
| Location | `docs/puml/` | `coding/docs/presentation/puml/` |

**Visual Optimization**:
- Thicker borders make elements visible from distance
- Larger fonts readable on projectors
- Horizontal layout fits 16:9 or 4:3 PPT slides
- Minimal text reduces cognitive load
- No legends/notes - slides should be self-explanatory or presenter explains

### Presentation Mode Example

**Original** (docs/puml/authentication-flow.puml):
- Vertical layout with detailed steps
- Includes notes about JWT validation
- Legend showing message types
- 12pt fonts, standard arrows

**Presentation** (coding/docs/presentation/puml/authentication-flow.puml):
- Horizontal left-to-right flow
- Only shows: User â†’ API â†’ Auth â†’ DB
- No notes or legends
- 18pt fonts, thick arrows (4pt)
- Labels: "Login", "Validate", "Query" (not "POST /api/v1/auth/login with credentials")

### Important Notes

- **Same filename**: Presentation versions use same name as original (no suffix)
- **Different location**: Stored in coding/docs/presentation/ tree
- **Not versioning**: This is a different presentation format, not a version
- **Reusable**: Presentation mode diagrams in coding/ can be used by all projects
- **Update both**: When updating a diagram, update both standard and presentation if needed

## Automation Opportunities

Consider creating helper scripts for:
- Batch validation of all .puml files
- Automated PNG generation on save
- Pre-commit hooks to enforce naming conventions
- Linting for incremental naming patterns
- Automatic presentation mode conversion
